Different Town hall levels are required before you can train footman, archer, gryphon, knights, paladin, siege tank and Dragons.\r\n\r\n\r\nGems\r\nAside from the game’s resources (gold, elixir), the game also uses gems as a currency. Gems may be used primarily to finish the time that certain processes take, such as the remaining time of a building’s or a troop’s upgrade, or to instantly train an army. \r\n\r\nControl\r\nPC Desktop, use mouse to select, move the building, zoom camera view. Click on the ground to unselect.\r\nXBOX One, use the controller left joystick to move the cursor and select with A button. Select any ground on the map to de-select.\r\n\r\nGuild\r\nBuild a guild house to enable this function. Enter guild to chat with other players.\r\n\r\nTravel \r\nBuild a Air depot to enable travel.\r\nTravel to other players castle to visit or loot.\r\n\r\nAttack\r\nSelect troop types ( more then 1 unit) and place on map, the troop will move and attack automatically.\r\n\r\nXBOX One, use the X button to launch troop. A Button to select.\r\n\r\nSetting\r\nSwitch game sound effects ON or OFF.\r\nSwitch game background music ON or OFF.\r\n\r\nHELP\r\nProvides quick start instructions.\r\n\r\nXBOX LIVE Services\r\n- XBOX Live Presence for friends and favourites\r\n- XBOX Live Global XP Leaderboard for Top 100 Ranking\r\n- XBOX Live Parental Service Controls enforcement for online communication, multiplayers and purchase.\r\n\r\nYouTube Promotio Trailer \r\nhttps://www.youtube.com/watch?v=9Pa4wvF4XIA\r\n\r\n---------------------------------------------------------\r\n\r\n\r\n","ProductFamilyName":"Games","Schema":"Card;1"}],"Title":"Mest populære betalte","HasThirdPartyIAPs":false,"AlgoName":"RECO-Algo-Version","AlgoValue":"Lists;topPaid;;Apps;00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000003","TotalItems":979,"PageSize":200}}
